A coding agent needs full analytical depth for correctness but should only expose high-level progress to avoid overwhelming the user. The solution is a structured two-tier format. The first tier is a compact user-facing progress block that updates incrementally. It tracks phase, current action, confidence, and next milestone. The second tier is a hidden or collapsible internal reasoning block that contains step-by-step logic, constraint checking, code generation rationale, error simulation, and self-correction. The agent parses the internal block to maintain state, then distills it into the external block. This architecture supports debugging, auditability, and clean UX. I will present it as a ready-to-use schema with clear boundaries between layers.Here is the designed format:**User-Facing Progress Block**```[PROGRESS]Phase: \u003canalysis|planning|implementing|testing|refining\u003eAction: \u003c1-line current step\u003eConfidence: \u003c0-100%\u003eNext: \u003c1-line upcoming step\u003eETA: \u003crelative time or milestone\u003e```**Internal Reasoning Block**```[REASONING]Context: \u003cproblem scope \u0026 constraints\u003eDecomposition: \u003clogical breakdown\u003eApproach: \u003calgorithm/library/structure choice\u003eEdge Cases: \u003cboundary conditions \u0026 failure modes\u003eCode Rationale: \u003cwhy this implementation\u003eSelf-Check: \u003cvalidation steps \u0026 corrections\u003eState Update: \u003cmemory/context carryover\u003e```**Usage Rules**- Always generate the internal block first, then distill it into the progress block.- Keep progress updates under5 lines; never expose raw chain-of-thought to the user.- Update confidence and phase dynamically based on self-check results.- Use the internal block for backtracking, alternative exploration, and silent error recovery.This structure ensures full analytical rigor while delivering clean, actionable status updates.","type":"response.output_text.done"}

A coding agent needs full analytical depth for correctness but should only expose high-level progress to avoid overwhelming the user. The solution is a structured two-tier format. The first tier is a compact user-facing progress block that updates incrementally. It tracks phase, current action, confidence, and next milestone. The second tier is a hidden or collapsible internal reasoning block that contains step-by-step logic, constraint checking, code generation rationale, error simulation, and self-correction. The agent parses the internal block to maintain state, then distills it into the external block. This architecture supports debugging, auditability, and clean UX. I will present it as a ready-to-use schema with clear boundaries between layers.Here is the designed format:**User-Facing Progress Block**```[PROGRESS]Phase: \u003canalysis|planning|implementing|testing|refining\u003eAction: \u003c1-line current step\u003eConfidence: \u003c0-100%\u003eNext: \u003c1-line upcoming step\u003eETA: \u003crelative time or milestone\u003e```**Internal Reasoning Block**```[REASONING]Context: \u003cproblem scope \u0026 constraints\u003eDecomposition: \u003clogical breakdown\u003eApproach: \u003calgorithm/library/structure choice\u003eEdge Cases: \u003cboundary conditions \u0026 failure modes\u003eCode Rationale: \u003cwhy this implementation\u003eSelf-Check: \u003cvalidation steps \u0026 corrections\u003eState Update: \u003cmemory/context carryover\u003e```**Usage Rules**- Always generate the internal block first, then distill it into the progress block.- Keep progress updates under5 lines; never expose raw chain-of-thought to the user.- Update confidence and phase dynamically based on self-check results.- Use the internal block for backtracking, alternative exploration, and silent error recovery.This structure ensures full analytical rigor while delivering clean, actionable status updates.","type":"output_text"},"response_id":"resp_chatcmpl-9krrTxf5uo8mK8XfVHbUydDKLtuQ84ay","sequence_number":1373,"type":"response.content_part.done"}

data: {"item":{"channel":"final","content":[{"text":"[SUMMARY]GOAL: Design a dual-layer reasoning format for coding agentsDECISION: Use a strict two-part template separating internal analysis from external progressNEXT: Present the template and usage rules conciselySTATUS: ready[DETAIL]The core challenge is balancing transparency with usability. A coding agent needs full analytical depth for correctness but should only expose high-level progress to avoid overwhelming the user. The solution is a structured two-tier format. The first tier is a compact user-facing progress block that updates incrementally. It tracks phase, current action, confidence, and next milestone. The second tier is a hidden or collapsible internal reasoning block that contains step-by-step logic, constraint checking, code generation rationale, error simulation, and self-correction. The agent parses the internal block to maintain state, then distills it into the external block. This architecture supports debugging, auditability, and clean UX.
